### Monarchism ###
	shared_focus = {
		id = JER_state_of_aquileia
		icon = GFX_goal_JER_state_of_aquileia
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = JER_fight_for_freedom }
		x = 4
		y = 0
		cost = 4.40
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
		allow_branch = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
						option = HIDE
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = JER_fight_for_freedom
				}
			}
		}
		select_effect = {
		    hidden_effect = {
			    set_global_flag = JER_monarchist_aquileia
			    country_event = {
				    id = aquileia.125
					days = 7
				}
		    }
	    }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_state_of_aquileia"
			add_political_power = 50
			custom_effect_tooltip = JER_revolution_tp
			hidden_effect = { #collapse focus tree
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = aquileian_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
			    if = {
			        limit = { has_character = JER_leonard_rodier }
			        JER_leonard_rodier = {
						remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					}
		        }
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

	shared_focus = {
		id = JER_help_rila
		icon = GFX_goal_JER_help_rila
		prerequisite = { focus = JER_state_of_aquileia }
		bypass = {
		    OR = {
		        has_global_flag = JER_revolution_begun
				has_global_flag = JER_revolution_ended
			}
		}
		x = -2
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = JER_state_of_aquileia
		cost = 7.20
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_help_rila"

			add_political_power = 60
			add_war_support = 0.025
			add_to_array = { JER_revolution_countries = JEB }
			set_variable = { JERrev_selected_country = JEB }
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

			custom_effect_tooltip = JER_increase_support_2
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_idea = civilian_economy
				}
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = civilian_economy
					add_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				}
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
					add_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			else = {
			    one_random_arms_factory = yes
			}
			add_manpower = -2500
			JEB = {
				country_event = {
					id = aquileia.2
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }
	}

	shared_focus = {
		id = JER_final_showdown
		icon = GFX_goal_JER_final_showdown
		prerequisite = { focus = JER_a_advisory_parliament }
		prerequisite = { focus = JER_reintegrate_old_lands }
		prerequisite = { focus = JER_the_grand_army }
		available = {
		    has_government = neutrality
			is_subject = no
			OR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						GRD = {
							OR = {
								tag = GRI
								tag = BRZ
								tag = ANG
								tag = FEA
								tag = KAT
								tag = PYT
								tag = ROU
								tag = TRD
								tag = YAL
								tag = STW
							}
						}
					}
					has_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
				}
                date > 1013.01.01
			}
		}
		bypass = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GRD
				tag = GRD
				AND = {
					GRD = { exists = no }
					382 = { owner = { has_war_with = ROOT } } #JER is already at war with the owner of Griffenheim
				}
				AND = {
					GRD = { exists = no }
					382 = { owns_or_subject_of = yes } #JER owns Griffenheim (directly or indirectly through a subject)
				}
			}
		}
		x = 0
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = JER_reintegrate_old_lands
		cost = 10.00
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 12
		}

		will_lead_to_war_with = GRD # tag alias for event_target:griffonian_empire
		will_lead_to_war_with = ANG
		will_lead_to_war_with = PYT
		will_lead_to_war_with = YAL
		will_lead_to_war_with = ROU
		will_lead_to_war_with = KAT
		will_lead_to_war_with = STW
		will_lead_to_war_with = BRZ
		will_lead_to_war_with = FEA

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_final_showdown"
			if = {
				limit = {
					GRD = { exists = yes }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = GRD
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = GRD
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { 382 = { owns_or_subject_of = yes } } #JER does not own Griffenheim (directly or indirectly through a subject)
					NOT = { 382 = { owner = { has_war_with = ROOT } } } #JER is not already at war with the owner of Griffenheim (in some weird case where GRD exists but the owner of 382 is not GRD, we want to declare on BOTH, which is why we're using this 'if' condition instead of an 'else' block a few lines earlier)
					NOT = { GRD = { exists = yes owns_state = 382 } } #if GRD exists and owns Griffenheim, then we're already declaring war on them in the above block
				}
				#JER declares war on the owner of Griffenheim
				hidden_effect = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = 382.owner
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = 382.owner
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FEA = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = FEA
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = FEA
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					STW = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							has_war_with = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					create_wargoal = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = STW
					}
				}
				declare_war_on = {
					type = annex_everything
					target = STW
				}
			}
			if = {

					ANG = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = {

			}

		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_develop_airplane_industry"
			add_resource = {
				type = aluminium
				amount = 10
				state = 407
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = aluminium
				amount = 12
				state = 406
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_tech = basic_medium_airframe
					}
					add_tech_bonus = {
						name = bomber_bonus
						bonus = 1.0
						uses = 1
						category = tactical_bomber
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = medium_plane_airframe
						amount = 50
						producer = JER
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_technology = {
